<Review>This is an awesome place run by good people and frequented by friendly locals with loads of information about the area. The store, while small, carries everything a thru-hiker might need for food supplies, plus frozen food and a microwave, and a pretty solid selection of beer. They're in the process of setting up a thru-hiker hostel, which is exactly what the area needs. For now, it's just bunkhouse, but they plan to add showers and laundry. < date>

< Rating>
5</Rating>
<text>One of the many great community benefits the Friends of the Dublin Library, a non-profit organization made up of local library-loving volunteers, offers is their three times per year Book Sales at the Dublin Library (March, September and December).

It's a great sale to help benefit and enhance the Dublin library. Definitely go if you love to read, listen to music or books or watch DVDs - children's, fiction, romance, mystery, health, foreign language, text books, gardening, cookbooks, science, art, etc. - CDs and DVDs, and audio books. You will find something to buy!

On the 2nd day of the March Sale (Sunday), they have a "$4 Bag Day Special." (As of March 2017). This allows you to fill up a grocery shopping bag for just $4. That day they have the Children's Books marked 50% off and CDs and DVDs at only 50 cents each!

Families love to come to these Friends of the Dublin Library Sales to stock up on their reading, music and DVD watching.

It was my first time to this type of Book Sale. I bought a $4 Bag and also filled up my reusable shopping bag full of Children's books and 9 CDs (classic rock, children's music, jazz, classical) for only $19!

In the Library next entrance, Friends of the Dublin Library has an area to browse and pay with either cash or check into a metal donation box throughout the year during Library hours. I scored on very good condition children's books at 50 cents each!< /text><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNlRHiaK9q_zvKMT9TqKQalGUcrKnoPjbK6kZdZ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNtKyOpDaBIgj6VHUb1gA0aHqzTjZGD38_Pnqrp=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNZFMQp47xSUxqWNRBiXP9AlgsgN8KtDE8w7EN5=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOCfuGsW-fL3GZCwDYPaOuoqAWUtdHEtLP8uf_p=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOFTI59skUGnPQ_i8YQCpFjgO0jUX_OdVeeQKGr=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pics><Response>None< /Response><Gmap_id>0x808fec0e6df6c1e7:0xd12bcf0bbc46b15e</Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

<review>I have never been more disappointed in an online coral dealer than I have with Reef Lounge USA. Initially, I was very excited to order from Reef Lounge due to some pretty great sales they had on their website and the chance for free shipping on orders over $300. Additionally, a reefer on Instagram supported their company so I figured I would give them a shot. I placed my order on a Wednesday and figured they might not ship it out until the following week because they only ship Monday-Wednesday. No worries there, I understand. I received my order confirmation email and they said they would update me with a tentative date they plan to ship my coral.

One week elapsed, and I still hadn't heard any updates from the company. Monday I expected an email, then Tuesday, then Wednesday- but nothing. So I called the shop and the lady who answered the phone was nice and told me my corals would be shipping out the next day, a Thursday. I was certainly confused because the website says they only ship Monday-Wednesday, but I was happy nonetheless to get an update at least.

Thursday came only to start the waves of disappointment with this company. First, I get an email stating that they JUST cut my frags, and they needed at least a week to heal, so they would not be shipping out like promised. Any online retailer I've purchased from before only sells pre cut frags, so it was disheartening to see they would be cutting my frags a week after I bought them. Then, 30 minutes later, I notice my bank account has been refunded the amount for my full order and I get an email from Reef Lounge stating that my order has been cancelled for no reason. EVERYTHING that I had purchased (on sale) was still listed as in stock on there website (no longer on sale of course), so I was very confused as to why the order would have been cancelled.

I reached out via email for clarification and to this day have not received an email back. I called 2 times, with a promise to have a call from customer service by the end of the day. I never received a call back. Finally, on my third call, a worker was able to give me an answer while belittling me in the process. He said, "See, this is coral- it is alive. If it dies after you buy it, we can't ship it so what would you like us to do? It is a living thing." The worker treated me as if I didn't know that I was buying livestock. I've been reefing for over 6 years and he mocks me as if I don't know the coral is living? Of course I understand that things can happen and coral may go out of stock. But to never communicate this (the fact that the coral you purchased has died before it even shipped) to the customer is a huge blunder. And no one has ever been able to explain how everything I ordered is still available on their site, yet magically when I ordered it on sale they no longer had any available to ship me?

I have had enough and will absolutely not order from this company. I would advise anyone else to do the same.<//review><date>1613437857330< /date><Rating>1< /Rating>< Response>

< Text>
VERY HELPFUL!!!! I live in New Hampshire and new to saltwater. I have a 15 gallon nano cube. The tank was set up for a pair of Hippocampus Erectus Seahorses. A few days after I brought them home one was laying on the sand. Eyes were moving normally. All the fish stores were closed because New Hampshire is eastern daylight time. I was panicked. My husband suggested that I call another State that is pacific daylight time. I went on line and found Reef Lounge USA listed and sells seahorses. The man I talked with was extremely knowledgeable and helpful. The fact that he knew he wouldn't get any business from me because of where I live didn't stop him from helping me. He asked what she was hitching to. Apparently what they hitch to will determine how they can hold themselves up. I was so relieved. I would highly recommend the Reef Lounge USA.< /Text>

<Resp>None</Resp>< review>
Place is great family owned and operated,  Jimmy (the owner) is very knowledgeable, and can answer any and every question you have.  I've read some of the other lower star reviews and almost don't believe it's the same store... Fish collection???  This is reef lounge,  maybe they have changed there name but I've been coming here for almost 2 years and it has been the best fish store I've ever been to.  I've purchased fish and taken them back the next day for a full refund/exchange. Not because they were sick but because my other fish were aggressive towards them.  I've had a red serpent star start to lose its limbs and was given full credit when I came in with what remained.  They have helped me solve a red algae problem,  and if I have any concerns about added something they give me stright answers. Often times telling me,  you can try but I wouldn't do it, or a flat out know you don't want this.  In fact I haven't had a single fish die from the store other the suicide because my flame hawk jumped out of the tank... Which they warned me about.  Anyone giving this place a one star knows nothing about the hobby and is probably upset because they didn't realize how expensive it can be and how difficult it is to maintain a nice healthy tank if your trying to do it cheap.  This place will tell you how to do it the right way,  at a fair and competitive price.  You might find something cheaper on Craigslist like one reviewer mentioned,  but it's CL and probably a scam... Though he didn't say how many bags of live sand he bought in his review but he did say he still got a $25 refund for some price matching.

I've been to other stores in the area,  and have had the owners just make you feel dumb for asking questions,  that will never happen here.  Id give it 6 stars if I could.<//review>

< Review>
My best friend and I (we‚Äôll call him X), had a huge passion and bond for saltwater reef and fish tanks. I had just acquired a custom 75 gallon tank that needed EVERYTHING, and X wanted to purchase a 150 gallon tank. In 2009 I was introduced to the owner of Reef Lounge Jimmy, by a friend who use to build custom tanks. X, bought a 180 gallon reef tank with everything from Reef Lounge, and the tank was beautiful, with beautiful fish and coral. X, Jimmy, and I maintained a business relationship for years. X maintained more of a friendship because Jimmy did monthly maintenance and cleaning. But as time went on the maintaining and cleaning started to slip.

April 2nd, 2016, I lost my best friend unexpectedly. His widow and children were of course in mourning, and his widow (knowing Jimmy was X‚Äôs friend) asked Jimmy to take the tank out of their home, and hold on to it until she and the children moved. She wanted to make the tank a memorial for her husband, something his children could enjoy, she could enjoy, and his friends could enjoy. X LOVED that stuff!

So this is what Jimmy did. Jimmy removed the tank from X‚Äôs home. He then resells the rock, fish, and corals to his employees because, ‚ÄúI had to pay my employees to move the tank‚Äù. Why wouldn‚Äôt he just bill the widow? For 2 hours of work his employees received 3 Kessil lights, a protein skimmer, refugium lighting, wave pumps, wave controller, chiller, and everything in the tank. Adding this up he paid his employees over $3000.00 to break down a tank (for a grieving widow) that took 2 hours.

I‚Äôm writing this review because that has to be the most unethical, sneakiest business man I‚Äôve ever met, and this story needs to be told. I went in there to look at the tank, it‚Äôs chipped, missing hardware. He has yet to speak to the widow. I‚Äôve let her know what happened to her husbands tank, and the unfortunate condition of what‚Äôs left of it. Where does she go from here, is of course, up to her, but felt what happened with Jimmy at Reef Lounge should be told. And I guess leave it up to you to decide if you want to deal with someone who could do that to someone at their lowest time.</Review>

1 Star meal: not even the manager, after issuing me a full refund, could tell me what this menu item was (no.9). Served warn, not hot. And bland, oh my was it bland.

1 Star service: I believe our server was given too many tables to serve. The result being I felt rushed, not heard, and in the end forgotten.

1 Star management: I had to come back twice to receive a refund. The first time I asked for a refund, the person in charge said I needed come back to speak with someone else.

When I came back the next day to see that person, to my dismay, the servers pointed out that same person I spoke with the other day. They said the guy I'm looking for is the one wearing the red shirt, sitting in the circle of men smoking cigars. Yep, it was the same guy from the day before. The same guy who told me I needed to speak to someone else. Well, he walked me back to the restaurant and gave me a refund.

I believe, depending on what day you go, what time of day or night you go, who is cooking that day or night, and how busy they are will determine the quality of the meal and level of service you will receive. Hence the wide range of reviewing experiences, all of which I believe true.</Review>

< text>
This is one of the few restaurants in Orange that my family and I will go to when we want to have a reliably good dinner. Everything, from the staff, casual atmosphere, and of course the delicious food is right on point. Just a heads up, there is a cigar store next door, and people will smoke out there, so you'll want to eat inside. We have never had to wait for a table inside, even when it's relatively busy. The portions are hefty enough for my wife and I to split a plate (we like the Sailor's Seafood Casserole). Delicious.</text>

<Text>Another Cuban restaurant that has lost what they once were.  Ever since the Father passed the manner in which they cut corners on cooking the food saddens me. Ramon we or I miss your dedication to making your customers happy with the quality of food and service<//Text>< pics>

<pics>None<//pics>< review>
I've eaten at Felix's for thirty years. It remains a very consistent restaurant, and one where the locals eat. A nice selection of meat, fish and chicken Cuban cuisine. Most meals begin about $13. For that one gets a hearty bowl of soup, or small salad, bread, the entree and one of three desserts. I like the plain Chicken Cubano, a half a roasted bird, a big helping of delicious rice, black beans and plantains. If you like a warm green sauce ask for it on the side. My wife enjoys the rice and chicken with vegetables. I do not eat meat, however traditional pork and beef dishes are plentiful on the menu. I like to pay for a slice of their homemade chocolate cake and then take home the dessert which comes with the meal for a snack the next day. Enjoy your meal with a drink of wine or a beer.

Try the breakfasts, many of which come with either a Tostada Latina, two slices of batter cooked french bread with a guava puree between, or the Fritter, a sort of cooked pastry ball with a sweet sauce. Most breakfasts are between $10 and $14. You can eat well for $10. Most breakfasts also include a small juice.

Service is good, people are nice and helpful. It's located in the Orange Circle. Parking is more easily found beyond the circle in several adjoining parking lots.

Try Felix's once and you'll likely return.<//review>

<name>dave mauzey</name>< user_id>
117550992030625172636< /user_id>
< Resp>
None<//Resp>
< text>
If you like cuban cuisine this might be a good place. It was crowded (which is a good sign)

Did not go inside, but that was mostly due to the cold temperatures outside and everyone was in there trying to get away from the cold air.
So we had to settle with outside and the heat lamps of which there were too few and not in good placement.

But if you like Spanish cuisine, im not so sure this is the one for you. My preference is PAELLA, I really know what works and what doesn't. The Paella (Valencia) in particular did not even come near my standards or even what is the standard to expect.

I know there are a lot of variations but this just was let me simply say this... NO!

The rice was more of a soggy mess, and was way too much. It overwhelmed the seafood and there was no socrate or socarrat. Speaking of seafood, (only one mussel), no clams (that I could make out), the shrimp was good (4), a few squid (no tentacles) and the fish was so mashed I could not find any decent pieces, the sausage (was more of a chorizo) had no business in there)

So if you like Paella don't eat that here, anything else perhaps but I will seek my dining in the downtown city of orange elsewhere and my Paella at other places I have been.</text>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures><Rate>3</Rate>< text>
This is a typical cafeteria style Cuban restaurant, the prices are fair and the food is fairly good.

On my last visit I was disappointed, I decided to try their paella, but found out that instead of using "imported spanish chorizo" like it is stated in their menu, they are using cheaper Mexican chorizo which is like night and day.

I mentioned this to the owner and he did not seem like he was going to lose any sleep over it, however he did ask if I wanted a different plate. It is a shame, a good paella deserves good Spanish chorizo.<//text>

< rate>
2</rate>
< review>
If you like cuban cuisine this might be a good place. It was crowded (which is a good sign)

Did not go inside, but that was mostly due to the cold temperatures outside and everyone was in there trying to get away from the cold air.
So we had to settle with outside and the heat lamps of which there were too few and not in good placement.

But if you like Spanish cuisine, im not so sure this is the one for you. My preference is PAELLA, I really know what works and what doesn't. The Paella (Valencia) in particular did not even come near my standards or even what is the standard to expect.

I know there are a lot of variations but this just was let me simply say this... NO!

The rice was more of a soggy mess, and was way too much. It overwhelmed the seafood and there was no socrate or socarrat. Speaking of seafood, (only one mussel), no clams (that I could make out), the shrimp was good (4), a few squid (no tentacles) and the fish was so mashed I could not find any decent pieces, the sausage (was more of a chorizo) had no business in there)

So if you like Paella don't eat that here, anything else perhaps but I will seek my dining in the downtown city of orange elsewhere and my Paella at other places I have been.<//review>
